Personal tech strategy for hybrid workforce Many employees are using their own devices for work, and we’re seeing a trend where people hold onto gadgets far beyond manufacturer recommendations. This creates security and reliability risks—older hardware often lacks updates, and repair costs start to outweigh replacement value. We recommend establishing a clear policy on minimum device specs and a 3-year rotation schedule. Otherwise, you’re just deferring costs into productivity loss.
